After the draw, the machine pays out if the hand or hands played match one of the winning combinations, which are posted in the pay table. \r\n\r\nPay tables allocate the payouts for hands and are based on how rare they are, the game variation, and the decision of the game operator. (Multi-play games are offered in \"Triple Play\", \"Five Play\", \"Ten Play\", \"Fifty Play\" and \"One Hundred Play\" versions.) \r\n\r\nIn games which do not have a wild card a player on average will receive the rare four-of-a-kind hand approximately once every 500 hands, while a player may play tens of thousands of hands before an extremely rare royal flush, which usually has the highest payout. \r\n\r\n\"Jacks or Better,\" sometimes simply called \"Draw Poker,\" is the most common variation of video poker.
